\doxysubsubsection*{Map}
These are convenience functions returning \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_map}{Map} objects. The \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a44523f8b49c90154f6195c6f04666499}{Map()} static functions return unaligned \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_map}{Map} objects, while the Aligned\+Map() functions return aligned \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_map}{Map} objects and thus should be called only with 16-\/byte-\/aligned {\itshape data} pointers.

Here is an example using strides\+:

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}

\end{DoxyVerbInclude}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+\_\+resize\+\_\+to\+\_\+match (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_ae6ea682fcdd15f8d93913c7b8b88557a}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!\_set@{\_set}}
\index{\_set@{\_set}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_set()}{\_set()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_ae6ea682fcdd15f8d93913c7b8b88557a} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::\+\_\+set (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [protected]}}



Copies the value of the expression {\itshape other} into {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} with automatic resizing. 

\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this might be resized to match the dimensions of {\itshape other}. If \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this was a null matrix (not already initialized), it will be initialized.

Note that copying a row-\/vector into a vector (and conversely) is allowed. The resizing, if any, is then done in the appropriate way so that row-\/vectors remain row-\/vectors and vectors remain vectors.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{参见}
operator=(const Matrix\+Base$<$\+Other\+Derived$>$\&), \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_aaa1298cf2d8f581e443f18a1b2296b5b}{\+\_\+set\+\_\+noalias()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a7f978b0b6cad676c9d01c2840f8113f5}{Scalar}} \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::coeff\+Ref (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{row\+Id}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{col\+Id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This is an overloaded version of Dense\+Coeffs\+Base$<$\+Derived,\+Write\+Accessors$>$\+::coeff\+Ref(\+Index,\+Index) const provided to by-\/pass the creation of an evaluator of the expression, thus saving compilation efforts.

See Dense\+Coeffs\+Base$<$\+Derived,\+Write\+Accessors$>$\+::coeff\+Ref(\+Index,\+Index) const for details. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_ae44be1764295d434bea1afca54fab261}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!coeffRef@{coeffRef}}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a7f978b0b6cad676c9d01c2840f8113f5}{Scalar}} \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::coeff\+Ref (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{row\+Id}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{col\+Id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::cols (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{conservativeResize()}{conservativeResize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a5e06c62950ba98fe8ba9c7d4be9c19e4} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::conservative\+Resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the matrix to {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} while leaving old values untouched.

The method is intended for matrices of dynamic size. If you only want to change the number of rows and/or of columns, you can use \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a46afa73816539b0fe36c6e9abd7978a6}{conservative\+Resize(\+No\+Change\+\_\+t, Index)} or \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a528879aef40f9cbc4ab4925e4a6bceb9}{conservative\+Resize(\+Index, No\+Change\+\_\+t)}.

Matrices are resized relative to the top-\/left element. In case values need to be appended to the matrix they will be uninitialized. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a528879aef40f9cbc4ab4925e4a6bceb9}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}}
\index{conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{conservativeResize()}{conservativeResize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a528879aef40f9cbc4ab4925e4a6bceb9} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::conservative\+Resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a57fe75444f853cd2dd2b6b94e27dcac7}{No\+Change\+\_\+t}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the matrix to {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} while leaving old values untouched.

As opposed to \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a5e06c62950ba98fe8ba9c7d4be9c19e4}{conservative\+Resize(\+Index rows, Index cols)}, this version leaves the number of columns unchanged.

In case the matrix is growing, new rows will be uninitialized. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a5429214e7c1ffaf7294a93a5cec62007}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}}
\index{conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{conservativeResize()}{conservativeResize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [3/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a5429214e7c1ffaf7294a93a5cec62007} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::conservative\+Resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the vector to {\itshape size} while retaining old values.

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors. This method does not work for partially dynamic matrices when the static dimension is anything other than 1. For example it will not work with \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix}{Matrix$<$double, 2, Dynamic$>$}.

When values are appended, they will be uninitialized. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a46afa73816539b0fe36c6e9abd7978a6}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}}
\index{conservativeResize@{conservativeResize}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{conservativeResize()}{conservativeResize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [4/4]}}

Resizes the matrix to {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} while leaving old values untouched.

As opposed to \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a5e06c62950ba98fe8ba9c7d4be9c19e4}{conservative\+Resize(\+Index rows, Index cols)}, this version leaves the number of rows unchanged.

In case the matrix is growing, new columns will be uninitialized. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a7775d274035c4ef541aa0fc9a3ad30a2}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!conservativeResizeLike@{conservativeResizeLike}}

template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::conservative\+Resize\+Like (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_dense_base}{Dense\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the matrix to {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} of {\ttfamily other}, while leaving old values untouched.

The method is intended for matrices of dynamic size. If you only want to change the number of rows and/or of columns, you can use \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a46afa73816539b0fe36c6e9abd7978a6}{conservative\+Resize(\+No\+Change\+\_\+t, Index)} or \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a528879aef40f9cbc4ab4925e4a6bceb9}{conservative\+Resize(\+Index, No\+Change\+\_\+t)}.

Matrices are resized relative to the top-\/left element. In case values need to be appended to the matrix they will copied from {\ttfamily other}. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a0df29d3bc898359bb3dc6bbd8d3cad12}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!data@{data}}

\index{operator=@{operator=}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{operator=()}{operator=()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/3]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a6cdc1003d9d60aefb01a66c4d3af389c} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::operator= (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Copies the generic expression {\itshape other} into \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this. 

The expression must provide a (templated) eval\+To(\+Derived\& dst) const function which does the actual job. In practice, this allows any user to write its own special matrix without having to modify \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix_base}{Matrix\+Base}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a reference to \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this.    
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a2ebcc910069dac4c4562e28db3893250}{Packet\+Scalar}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::packet (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{row\+Id}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{col\+Id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

\Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!resize@{resize}}
\index{resize@{resize}!Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{resize()}{resize()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a99d9054ee2d5a40c6e00ded0265e9cea} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} to a {\itshape rows} x {\itshape cols} matrix.

This method is intended for dynamic-\/size matrices, although it is legal to call it on any matrix as long as fixed dimensions are left unchanged. If you only want to change the number of rows and/or of columns, you can use \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_ab71a655f73d05a0e389e3ed13b6fe5f3}{resize(\+No\+Change\+\_\+t, Index)}, \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a7b44761b7350ae3756035bbf7d7c04f6}{resize(\+Index, No\+Change\+\_\+t)}.

If the current number of coefficients of {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} exactly matches the product {\itshape rows} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} {\itshape cols}, then no memory allocation is performed and the current values are left unchanged. In all other cases, including shrinking, the data is reallocated and all previous values are lost.

Example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCodeInclude}{0}

\end{DoxyCodeInclude}
 Output\+: 
\begin{DoxyVerbInclude}
\end{DoxyVerbInclude}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_a7b44761b7350ae3756035bbf7d7c04f6} 
template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_eigen_a57fe75444f853cd2dd2b6b94e27dcac7}{No\+Change\+\_\+t}}}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes the matrix, changing only the number of rows. For the parameter of type \doxylink{namespace_eigen_a57fe75444f853cd2dd2b6b94e27dcac7}{No\+Change\+\_\+t}, just pass the special value {\ttfamily No\+Change} as in the example below.

EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{size}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} to a vector of length {\itshape size} 

\textbackslash{}only\+\_\+for\+\_\+vectors. This method does not work for partially dynamic matrices when the static dimension is anything other than 1. For example it will not work with \doxylink{class_eigen_1_1_matrix}{Matrix$<$double, 2, Dynamic$>$}.

template$<$typename Other\+Derived$>$ \\
EIGEN\+\_\+\+DEVICE\+\_\+\+FUNC \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::resize\+Like (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_eigen_1_1_eigen_base}{Eigen\+Base}}$<$ Other\+Derived $>$ \&}]{\+\_\+other}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

Resizes {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}this} to have the same dimensions as {\itshape other}. Takes care of doing all the checking that\textquotesingle{}s needed.

Note that copying a row-\/vector into a vector (and conversely) is allowed. The resizing, if any, is then done in the appropriate way so that row-\/vectors remain row-\/vectors and vectors remain vectors. \Hypertarget{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base_aba7a925ce36c08ba2a08c90086f34718}\index{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$@{Eigen::PlainObjectBase$<$ Derived $>$}!rows@{rows}}

template$<$typename Derived$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{eigen-3_83_87_2_eigen_2src_2_core_2util_2_macros_8h_af2b60117c00a6e75812de43bfe7db3b1}{EIGEN\+\_\+\+STRONG\+\_\+\+INLINE}} Derived \& \mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_plain_object_base}{Eigen\+::\+Plain\+Object\+Base}}$<$ Derived $>$\+::set\+Random (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{rows}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{class_eigen_1_1_tensor}{Index}}}]{cols}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Resizes to the given size, and sets all coefficients in this expression to random values.

\doxylink{example__custom__name_8cpp_a2c973620a3fe7f923747ed2baa1bae4e}{Numbers} are uniformly spread through their whole definition range for integer types, and in the \mbox{[}-\/1\+:1\mbox{]} range for floating point scalar types.

\textbackslash{}not\+\_\+reentrant

{\em rows} & the new number of rows \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
